NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE.

I, CT. Aswin Lakshman, son of Thiru L. Chidambaram & CT. Saroja, born on 4th January 1988 was adopted by
Thiru RM. Sevagan Chettiyar & SP Lakshmi vide adoption deed No.116/2012, dated 24th May 2012 with the name of
SV. RAMANATHAN and the same was published in TNGG No. 14 of April 2013. The Adoption has now been
mutually cancelled vide lok adalat case OS No 63 of 2016 and shall henceforth be known by my previous name
as CT. ASWIN LAKSHMAN hereafter.
Chennai,
18th August 2016.

SV. RAMANATHAN.

S. Muthumari, a Female Child born to V. Suresh Narayanan on 9th July 1989 residing at No. 128, Subramaniyapuram,

Thoothukudi,
